    MxGraph.prototype.insertCell = function (grph, evt, target, x, y) {
        var test = this.state.test;
        var cell = new mxCell(test, new mxGeometry(0, 0, 80, 30));
        cell.vertex = true;
        var cells = grph.importCells([cell], x, y, target);
        if (cells != null && cells.length > 0) {
            grph.scrollCellToVisible(cells[0]);
            grph.setSelectionCells(cells);
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.setDragElement = function (dragid) {
        this.setState(function () { return ({
            dragElement: document.getElementById(dragid)
        }); });
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.initiateDragPreview = function () {
        // Creates the element that is being for the actual preview.
        var dragElt = document.createElement('div');
        dragElt.style.border = 'dashed black 1px';
        dragElt.style.width = '80px';
        dragElt.style.height = '30px';
        this.setState(function () { return ({
            preview: dragElt,
        }); });
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.getGraphUnderMouse = function (evt) {
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        var x = mxEvent.getClientX(evt);
        var y = mxEvent.getClientY(evt);
        var elt = document.elementFromPoint(x, y);
        if (mxUtils.isAncestorNode(graph.container, elt)) {
            return graph;
        }
        return null;
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.makeDragSource = function (dragElement) {
        var preview = this.state.preview;
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        var ds = mxUtils.makeDraggable(dragElement, this.getGraphUnderMouse, this.insertCell, preview, null, null, graph.autoscroll, true);
        // Redirects feature to global switch. Note that this feature should only be used
        // if the the x and y arguments are used in funct to insert the cell.
        ds.isGuidesEnabled = function () {
            return graph.graphHandler.guidesEnabled;
        };
        // Restores original drag icon while outside of graph
        ds.createDragElement = mxDragSource.prototype.createDragElement;
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.handleLoad = function () {
        this.main(document.getElementById('graphContainer'));
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.saveGraph = function (g) {
        this.setState({
            graph: g
        });
    };

    MxGraph.prototype.extendCanvas = function (graph) {
        /**
         * Specifies the size of the size for "tiles" to be used for a graph with
         * scrollbars but no visible background page. A good value is large
         * enough to reduce the number of repaints that is caused for auto-
         * translation, which depends on this value, and small enough to give
         * a small empty buffer around the graph. Default is 400x400.
         */
        graph.scrollTileSize = new mxRectangle(0, 0, 400, 400);
        /**
         * Returns the padding for pages in page view with scrollbars.
         */
        graph.getPagePadding = function () {
            return new mxPoint(Math.max(0, Math.round(graph.container.offsetWidth - 34)), Math.max(0, Math.round(graph.container.offsetHeight - 34)));
        };
        /**
         * Returns the size of the page format scaled with the page size.
         */
        graph.getPageSize = function () {
            return (this.pageVisible) ?
                new mxRectangle(0, 0, this.pageFormat.width * this.pageScale, this.pageFormat.height * this.pageScale)
                : this.scrollTileSize;
        };
        /**
         * Returns a rectangle describing the position and count of the
         * background pages, where x and y are the position of the top,
         * left page and width and height are the vertical and horizontal
         * page count.
         */
        graph.getPageLayout = function () {
            var size = (this.pageVisible) ? this.getPageSize() : this.scrollTileSize;
            var bounds = this.getGraphBounds();
            if (bounds.width === 0 || bounds.height === 0) {
                return new mxRectangle(0, 0, 1, 1);
            }
            else {
                // Computes untransformed graph bounds
                var x = Math.ceil(bounds.x / this.view.scale - this.view.translate.x);
                var y = Math.ceil(bounds.y / this.view.scale - this.view.translate.y);
                var w = Math.floor(bounds.width / this.view.scale);
                var h = Math.floor(bounds.height / this.view.scale);
                var x0 = Math.floor(x / size.width);
                var y0 = Math.floor(y / size.height);
                var w0 = Math.ceil((x + w) / size.width) - x0;
                var h0 = Math.ceil((y + h) / size.height) - y0;
                return new mxRectangle(x0, y0, w0, h0);
            }
        };
        // Fits the number of background pages to the graph
        graph.view.getBackgroundPageBounds = function () {
            var layout = this.graph.getPageLayout();
            var page = this.graph.getPageSize();
            return new mxRectangle(this.scale * (this.translate.x + layout.x * page.width), this.scale * (this.translate.y + layout.y * page.height), this.scale * layout.width * page.width, this.scale * layout.height * page.height);
        };
        graph.getPreferredPageSize = function () {
            var pages = this.getPageLayout();
            var size = this.getPageSize();
            return new mxRectangle(0, 0, pages.width * size.width, pages.height * size.height);
        };
        /**
         * THIS FUNCTION CAUSED AUTOFOCUS BUG !!!!
         */

            console.log("graphViewValidate");

                let pad = this.graph.getPagePadding();
                let size = this.graph.getPageSize();
 
                // Updating scrollbars here causes flickering in quirks and is not needed
                // if zoom method is always used to set the current scale on the graph.
                this.translate.x = pad.x / this.scale - (this.x0 || 0) * size.width;
                this.translate.y = pad.y / this.scale - (this.y0 || 0) * size.height;
            }
 
            graphViewValidate.apply(this, arguments);
        };*/
        var graphSizeDidChange = graph.sizeDidChange;
        graph.sizeDidChange = function () {
            if (this.container !== null && mxUtils.hasScrollbars(this.container)) {
                var pages = this.getPageLayout();
                var pad = this.getPagePadding();
                var size = this.getPageSize();
                // Updates the minimum graph size
                var minw = Math.ceil(2 * pad.x / this.view.scale + pages.width * size.width);
                var minh = Math.ceil(2 * pad.y / this.view.scale + pages.height * size.height);
                var min = graph.minimumGraphSize;
                // LATER: Fix flicker of scrollbar size in IE quirks mode
                // after delayed call in window.resize event handler
                if (min === null || min.width !== minw || min.height !== minh) {
                    graph.minimumGraphSize = new mxRectangle(0, 0, minw, minh);
                }
                // Updates auto-translate to include padding and graph size
                var dx = pad.x / this.view.scale - pages.x * size.width;
                var dy = pad.y / this.view.scale - pages.y * size.height;
                if (!this.autoTranslate && (this.view.translate.x !== dx || this.view.translate.y !== dy)) {
                    this.autoTranslate = true;
                    this.view.x0 = pages.x;
                    this.view.y0 = pages.y;
                    // NOTE: THIS INVOKES THIS METHOD AGAIN. UNFORTUNATELY THERE IS NO WAY AROUND THIS SINCE THE
                    // BOUNDS ARE KNOWN AFTER THE VALIDATION AND SETTING THE TRANSLATE TRIGGERS A REVALIDATION.
                    // SHOULD MOVE TRANSLATE/SCALE TO VIEW.
                    var tx = graph.view.translate.x;
                    var ty = graph.view.translate.y;
                    graph.view.setTranslate(dx, dy);
                    graph.container.scrollLeft += (dx - tx) * graph.view.scale;
                    graph.container.scrollTop += (dy - ty) * graph.view.scale;
                    this.autoTranslate = false;
                    return;
                }
                graphSizeDidChange.apply(this, arguments);
            }
        };
        // Sets initial scrollbar positions
        window.setTimeout(function () {
            var bounds = graph.getGraphBounds();
            var width = Math.max(bounds.width, graph.scrollTileSize.width * graph.view.scale);
            var height = Math.max(bounds.height, graph.scrollTileSize.height * graph.view.scale);
            graph.container.scrollTop =
                Math.floor(Math.max(0, bounds.y - Math.max(20, (graph.container.clientHeight - height) / 4)));
            graph.container.scrollLeft =
                Math.floor(Math.max(0, bounds.x - Math.max(0, (graph.container.clientWidth - width) / 2)));
        }, 0);
    };
    /* ALT + SCROLL: zoom, ALT: panning */
    MxGraph.prototype.initPeripheralHandling = function (graph) {
        // // Adds mouse wheel handling for zoom
        mxEvent.addMouseWheelListener(function (evt, up) {
            if (up && evt.altKey) {
                graph.zoomIn();
                mxEvent.consume(evt);
            }
            else if (evt.altKey) {
                graph.zoomOut();
                mxEvent.consume(evt);
            }
        });
        document.onkeydown = function (evt) {
            if (evt.altKey) {
                graph.panningHandler.ignoreCell = true;
            }
        };
        document.onkeyup = function () {
            graph.panningHandler.ignoreCell = false;
        };
        graph.panningHandler.addListener(mxEvent.PAN, function () {
            graph.container.style.cursor = 'move';
        });
        graph.panningHandler.addListener(mxEvent.PAN_START, function () {
            graph.container.style.cursor = 'move';
        });
        graph.panningHandler.addListener(mxEvent.PAN_END, function () {
            graph.container.style.cursor = 'default';
        });
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.configureCells = function (editor, graph) {
        editor.layoutSwimlanes = true;
        editor.createSwimlaneLayout = function () {
            var layout = new mxStackLayout(this.graph, false);
            layout.fill = true;
            layout.resizeParent = true;
            // Overrides the function to always return true
            layout.isVertexMovable = function () {
                return true;
            };
            return layout;
        };
        // Only shapes/tables are movable
        graph.isCellMovable = function (cell) {
            return this.isSwimlane(cell);
        };
        // Only shapes/tables are resizable, this fixes the style
        graph.isCellResizable = function (cell) {
            return this.isSwimlane(cell);
        };
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.configureLabels = function (graph) {
        // Returns the name field of the user object for the label
        graph.convertValueToString = function (cell) {
            if (cell.value != null && cell.value.name != null) {
                return cell.value.name;
            }
            // "supercall"
            return mxGraph.prototype.convertValueToString.apply(this, arguments);
        };
        // let superCellLabelChanged = graph.cellLabelChanged;
        // graph.cellLabelChanged = function (cell: any, newValue: string, autoSize: any) {
        //     console.log(cell, newValue);
        //     // if (cell.value) {
        //     //     // Clones the value for correct undo/redo
        //     //     // let elt = mxUtils.clone(cell.value);
        //     //     let elt = cell.value.clone();
        //     //     elt.setAttribute('name', newValue);
        //     //     newValue = elt;
        //     // }
        //     superCellLabelChanged.apply(this, arguments);
        // };
        graph.getLabel = function (cell) {
            if (this.isHtmlLabel(cell)) {
                return mxUtils.htmlEntities(cell.value.name);
            }
            return mxGraph.prototype.getLabel.apply(this, arguments);
        };
        var instance = this;
        // Text label changes will go into the name field of the user object
        graph.model.valueForCellChanged = function (cell, value) {
            var triple = instance.cellToTriples.getValue(cell);
            if (triple && cell.style === "Row") {
                var _a = value.split(" : ").map(function (d) { return d.trim(); }), predicate = _a[0], object = _a[1];
                var newTriple = new Triple(triple.object, predicate, object, triple.file);
                instance.editTriple(cell, triple, newTriple);
            }
            else {
                // instance.editBlock(cell, value);
                console.log('Edit blocking');
            }
            if (value.name != null) {
                return mxGraphModel.prototype.valueForCellChanged.apply(this, arguments);
            }
            else {
                var old = cell.value.name;
                cell.value.name = value;
                return old;
            }
        };
        // Properties are dynamically created HTML labels
        // Returns true for properties and false for shapes
        graph.isHtmlLabel = function (cell) {
            return !this.isSwimlane(cell) && !this.model.isEdge(cell);
        };
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.configureTooltips = function (graph) {
        // Installs a custom global tooltip
        graph.setTooltips(true);
        graph.getTooltip = function (state) {
            var cell = state.cell;
            // If the cell is invalid, then it will have an error
            // thus display the error message, else just show the label
            if (cell.value.error) {
                return cell.value.error.toString();
            }
            else {
                return graph.getLabel(cell);
            }
        };
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.initStandardCells = function () {
        var blockObject = new Block();
        var block = new mxCell(blockObject, new mxGeometry(0, 0, 250, 28));
        block.setVertex(true);
        this.nameToStandardCellDict.setValue('block', block);
        var rowObject = new Row();
        var row = new mxCell(rowObject, new mxGeometry(0, 0, 0, 26), 'Row');
        row.setVertex(true);
        row.setConnectable(false);
        this.nameToStandardCellDict.setValue('row', row);
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.addNewRowOverlay = function (graph, cell) {
        // Creates a new overlay in the middle with an image and a tooltip
        var overlay = new mxCellOverlay(new mxImage('img/add.png', 24, 24), 'Add a new row', mxConstants.ALIGN_CENTER);
        overlay.cursor = 'hand';
        var model = graph.getModel();
        var instance = this;
        var temprow = model.cloneCell(instance.nameToStandardCellDict.getValue('row'));
        var blockName, trait, triple;
        // Installs a handler for clicks on the overlay
        overlay.addListener(mxEvent.CLICK, function (sender, event) {
            graph.clearSelection();
            model.beginUpdate();
            try {
                blockName = event.properties.cell.value.realName;
                // here the assumption is made that next row will belong to the same file as the first
                // we just need to make sure that there is at least one row as well
                // this also makes sense since a node without rows is pointless
                trait = instance.cellToTriples.getValue(event.properties.cell.children[0]);
                if (trait) {
                    triple = new Triple(blockName, "predicate", "object", trait.file);
                    temprow.value.name = instance.nameFromTrait(triple);
                    cell.insert(temprow);
                }
            }
            finally {
                // Updates the display
                model.endUpdate();
                graph.refresh();
            }
        });
        if (triple) {
            // start an update task in the model
            var file = triple.file;
            var oldGraph = instance.fileToGraphDict.getValue(file);
            var type = instance.fileToTypeDict.getValue(file);
            if (oldGraph && type) {
                var backendModel = dataAccessProvider_1.DataAccessProvider.getInstance().model;
                var newGraph = oldGraph.addTriple(triple.subject, triple.predicate, triple.object);
                backendModel.tasks.schedule(new ModelTasks_1.EditTriple(newGraph, type, file));
                // TODO remove this after testing
                backendModel.tasks.processAllTasks();
            }
            else {
                console.log("error: graph or type undefined");
            }
            // update the data structures
            instance.triples.add(triple);
            instance.cellToTriples.setValue(temprow, triple);
            var block = instance.subjectToBlockDict.getValue(blockName);
            if (block) {
                block.traits.push(triple);
            }
            else {
                console.log("error: could not find block: " + blockName);
            }
            console.log(block);
        }
        // Sets the overlay for the cell in the graph
        graph.addCellOverlay(cell, overlay);
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.parseDataGraphToBlocks = function (persistenceGraph, file) {
        var _this = this;
        var RDF = $rdf.Namespace("http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#");
        var SH = $rdf.Namespace("http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#");
        var triples = persistenceGraph.query(function (store) { return store; }).statements;
        this.fileToGraphDict.setValue(file, persistenceGraph);
        var newTriples = new Collections.Set();
        triples.forEach(function (triple) {
            if (!_this.subjectToBlockDict.containsKey(triple.subject.value)) {
                _this.subjectToBlockDict.setValue(triple.subject.value, new Block(triple.subject.value));
            }
            newTriples.add(new Triple(triple.subject.value, triple.predicate.value, triple.object.value, file));
        });
        newTriples.difference(this.triples);
        this.triples.union(newTriples);
        this.needToRender = !newTriples.isEmpty();
        newTriples.forEach(function (triple) {
            var subject = triple.subject;
            var predicate = triple.predicate;
            var object = triple.object;
            var subjectBlock = _this.subjectToBlockDict.getValue(subject);
            if (subjectBlock) {
                if (predicate === RDF("type").uri && object === SH("NodeShape").uri) {
                    subjectBlock.blockType = "NodeShape";
                    subjectBlock.triple = triple;
                }
                else if (predicate === SH("path").uri) {
                    subjectBlock.name = object;
                    subjectBlock.realName = subject;
                    subjectBlock.blockType = "Property";
                    subjectBlock.triple = triple;
                }
                else {
                    subjectBlock.traits.push(triple);
                }
            }
        });
        return this.subjectToBlockDict.values();
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.clear = function () {
        this.blockToCellDict.clear();
        this.cellToTriples.clear();
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        graph.removeCells(graph.getChildVertices(graph.getDefaultParent()));
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.visualizeFile = function (persistenceGraph, type, file, prefixes) {
        var _this = this;
        var blocks = this.parseDataGraphToBlocks(persistenceGraph, file);
        if (!this.needToRender) {
            return;
        }
        this.clear();
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        this.fileToTypeDict.setValue(file, type);
        var model = graph.getModel();
        var parent = graph.getDefaultParent();
        blocks.forEach(function (b) {
            b.name = _this.replacePrefixes(b.name, prefixes);
            var v1 = model.cloneCell(_this.nameToStandardCellDict.getValue('block'));
            v1.value.name = b.name;
            v1.value.realName = b.realName;
            _this.blockToCellDict.setValue(b, v1);
        });
        blocks.forEach(function (b) {
            var blockCell = _this.blockToCellDict.getValue(b);
            model.beginUpdate();
            var rows = []; // store rows temporarily, since they only get an id after the model updates
            try {
                var longestname_1 = 0;
                b.traits.forEach(function (trait) {
                    var rowCell = model.cloneCell(_this.nameToStandardCellDict.getValue('row'));
                    var name = _this.nameFromTrait(trait, prefixes);
                    longestname_1 = Math.max(name.length, longestname_1);
                    rowCell.value.name = name;
                    blockCell.insert(rowCell);
                    var b2 = _this.subjectToBlockDict.getValue(trait.object);
                    if (b2) {
                        var v2 = _this.blockToCellDict.getValue(b2);
                        graph.insertEdge(graph.getDefaultParent(), null, '', rowCell, v2);
                    }
                    rows.push(rowCell);
                });
                _this.addNewRowOverlay(graph, blockCell);
                if (!b.blockType) {
                    b.blockType = "Data";
                }
                blockCell.value.blockType = b.blockType;
                blockCell.style = b.blockType;
                blockCell.geometry.width += longestname_1 * 4;
                blockCell.geometry.alternateBounds =
                    new mxRectangle(0, 0, blockCell.geometry.width, blockCell.geometry.height);
                graph.addCell(blockCell, parent);
            }
            finally {
                model.endUpdate();
            }
            for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
                _this.cellToTriples.setValue(rows[i], b.traits[i]);
                b.traits[i].cell = rows[i];
            }
            if (b.triple) {
                _this.cellToTriples.setValue(blockCell, b.triple);
                b.triple.cell = blockCell;
            }
        });
        var layout = new mxStackLayout(graph, false, 35);
        layout.execute(graph.getDefaultParent());
    };
    /**
     * Get the name for a row based on trait
     */
    MxGraph.prototype.nameFromTrait = function (trait, prefixes) {
        if (prefixes) {
            return this.replacePrefixes(trait.predicate, prefixes)
                + " :  "
                + this.replacePrefixes(trait.object, prefixes);
        }
        else {
            return trait.predicate + " : " + trait.object;
        }
    };
    /**
     * Replaces prefixes where possible in the string s
     * @param {string} s
     * @param {PrefixMap} prefixes
     */
    MxGraph.prototype.replacePrefixes = function (s, prefixes) {
        Object.keys(prefixes).forEach(function (key) {
            s = s.replace(prefixes[key], key + ":");
        });
        return s;
    };

    };
    MxGraph.prototype.initDragAndDrop = function (graph) {
        var sidebar = document.getElementById("sideBarID");
        for (var _i = 0, _a = this.state.dragElList; _i < _a.length; _i++) {
            var id = _a[_i];
            this.addDraggableElement(graph, sidebar, id);
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.addDraggableElement = function (graph, sidebar, id) {
        // Function that is executed when the image is dropped on
        // the graph. The cell argument points to the cell under
        // the mousepointer if there is one.
        var model = graph.getModel();
        var block = this.nameToStandardCellDict.getValue('block');
        var row = this.nameToStandardCellDict.getValue('row');
        var funct = function (g, evt, target, x, y) {
            var v1 = model.cloneCell(block);
            var parent = graph.getDefaultParent();
            /* Set correct styling based on input */
            var style = 'NodeShape';
            if (id.indexOf('Property') >= 0) {
                style = 'Property';
            }
            /* Create empty block */
            var b = v1.getValue();
            b.name = "new " + id;
            b.blockType = style;
            /* Create empty row */
            var temprow = model.cloneCell(row);
            b.traits = [];
            model.beginUpdate();
            try {
                v1.insert(temprow);
                v1.style = style;
                v1.geometry.x = x;
                v1.geometry.y = y;
                v1.geometry.width += 10 * 4;
                graph.addCell(v1, parent);
                v1.geometry.alternateBounds =
                    new mxRectangle(0, 0, v1.geometry.width, v1.geometry.height);
            }
            finally {
                // Updates the display
                model.endUpdate();
            }
            graph.setSelectionCell(v1);
        };
        // Creates the compoent which is used as the draggabmle element (drag source)
        var comp = document.getElementById(String(id));
        /* Create draggable element */
        var ds = mxUtils.makeDraggable(comp, graph, funct);
        ds.isGuidesEnabled = function () {
            return graph.graphHandler.guidesEnabled;
        };
        // Restores original drag icon while outside of graph
        ds.createDragElement = mxDragSource.prototype.createDragElement;
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.addTemplate = function () {
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        var templateCount = this.state.templateCount;
        // TODO: prevent multiple cell selection
        // TODO: positioning??
        if (!graph.isSelectionEmpty()) {
            // Creates a copy of the selection array to preserve its state
            var cells = graph.getSelectionCells();
            // var bounds = graph.getView().getBounds(cells);
            console.log(cells);
            console.log(cells[0].value);
            var cellname = void 0;
            // handle multiple cell selection
            if (cells.length === 1) {
                // handle non-block/block cells differently
                if (typeof (cells[0].value) === "string") {
                    cellname = cells[0].value;
                }
                else {
                    cellname = cells[0].value.name.split("/").pop();
                    console.log(cells[0]);
                    // set all block clear all block values
                    cells[0].value.traits = [];
                }
            }
            else {
                cellname = "Multiple components";
            }
            // Function that is executed when the image is dropped on
            // the graph. The cell argument points to the cell under
            // the mousepointer if there is one.
            var funct = function (gr, evt, target, x, y, cell) {
                gr.setSelectionCells(gr.importCells(cells, x, y, cell));
            };
            // create sidebar entry
            // invoke callback on parent component, which will add entry to sidebar
            this.props.callback(cellname, templateCount);
            // increment state counter
            this.setState({
                templateCount: templateCount + 1
            });
            // let preview = null;
            var drag = document.getElementById(cellname + templateCount);
            mxUtils.makeDraggable(drag, graph, funct);
            this.props.setLabel(false);
        }
        else {
            console.log("nothing is selected");
            this.props.setLabel(true);
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.main = function (container) {
        var _this = this;
        // TODO remove after test
        var ps = new PollingService_1.default(5000);
        ps.startPolling();
        // Checks if the browser is supported
        if (!container) {
            mxUtils.error('Could not find \'graphContainer\'', 200, false);
        }
        else if (!mxClient.isBrowserSupported()) {
            mxUtils.error('Browser is not supported!', 200, false);
        }
        else {
            var model_2 = dataAccessProvider_1.DataAccessProvider.getInstance().model;
            model_2.registerObserver(new model_1.ModelObserver(function (changeBuf) {
                var tasks = new Array();
                changeBuf.forEach(function (key) {
                    // only listen to IO, mgxgraph handles the other changes
                    if (key === modelTaskMetadata_1.ModelComponent.IO) {
                        // TODO only one task with both
                        tasks.push(new ModelTasks_1.VisualizeComponent(modelTaskMetadata_1.ModelComponent.DataGraph, _this));
                        tasks.push(new ModelTasks_1.VisualizeComponent(modelTaskMetadata_1.ModelComponent.SHACLShapesGraph, _this));
                    }
                });
                return tasks;
            }));
            // listen to all click events and key pressed events to check if user is actively editing
            document.addEventListener("click", this.handleUserAction, true);
            document.addEventListener("keypress", this.handleUserAction, true);
            var editor = new mxEditor();
            // Creates the graph inside the given container
            editor.setGraphContainer(container);
            var graph = editor.graph;
            // Set keyboard short cuts
            var kbsc = require('./config/keyhandler-minimal.xml');
            var config = mxUtils.load(kbsc).getDocumentElement();
            editor.configure(config);
            // Enable Panning
            graph.panningHandler.ignoreCell = false;
            graph.setPanning(true);
            this.extendCanvas(graph);
            new mxRubberband(graph); // Enables rubberband selection
            this.initPeripheralHandling(graph);
            this.configureStylesheet(graph);
            this.configureCells(editor, graph);
            this.configureLabels(graph);
            this.configureTooltips(graph);
            this.initStandardCells();
            this.saveGraph(graph);
            this.initiateDragPreview();
            this.initDragAndDrop(graph);
            this.initToolBar(editor);
            container.focus();
            // Get add template button
            var d2 = document.getElementById("addTemplate");
            if (d2) {
                d2.onclick = this.addTemplate;
            }
            graph.addListener(mxEvent.CELLS_REMOVED, function (sender, evt) {
                var cells = evt.getProperty("cells");
                for (var i = 0; i < cells.length; i++) {
                    var cell = cells[i];
                    var triple = _this.cellToTriples.getValue(cell);
                    if (triple && cell.style === "Row") {
                        // a row was removed
                        _this.removeTriple(triple, model_2);
                    }
                    else if (_this.blockToCellDict.containsKey(cell.value)) {
                        // a block was removed
                        var block = _this.subjectToBlockDict.getValue(cell.value.realName);
                        if (block) {
                            if (block.triple) {
                                // block is a property or shape, not data
                                _this.removeTriple(block.triple, model_2);
                            }
                            for (var _i = 0, _a = block.traits; _i < _a.length; _i++) {
                                var trait = _a[_i];
                                _this.removeTriple(trait, model_2);
                            }
                            _this.subjectToBlockDict.remove(block.realName);
                            _this.blockToCellDict.remove(block);
                        }
                    }
                }
                _this.debug();
            });
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.debug = function () {
        console.log(this.blockToCellDict);
        console.log(this.subjectToBlockDict);
        console.log(this.triples);
        console.log(this.cellToTriples);
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.removeTriple = function (triple, model) {
        this.removeTripleFromBlocks(triple);
        this.triples.remove(triple);
        this.cellToTriples.remove(triple.cell);
        this.removeTripleFromModel(triple, model);
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.removeTripleFromModel = function (triple, model) {
        var oldGraph = this.fileToGraphDict.getValue(triple.file);
        var type = this.fileToTypeDict.getValue(triple.file);
        if (oldGraph && type) {
            console.log(triple.subject, triple.predicate, triple.object);
            var newGraph = oldGraph.removeTriple(triple.subject, triple.predicate, triple.object);
            this.fileToGraphDict.setValue(triple.file, newGraph);
            model.tasks.schedule(new ModelTasks_1.EditTriple(newGraph, type, triple.file));
            model.tasks.processAllTasks();
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.editTriple = function (cell, oldTriple, newTriple) {
        var model = dataAccessProvider_1.DataAccessProvider.getInstance().model;
        // Update data structures
        this.triples.remove(oldTriple);
        this.triples.add(newTriple);
        this.cellToTriples.setValue(cell, newTriple);
        // Edit triple in the model
        var oldGraph = this.fileToGraphDict.getValue(newTriple.file);
        var file = this.fileToTypeDict.getValue(newTriple.file);
        if (oldGraph && file) {
            // Use param object to adhere to interface of the backend graph structure
            var param = { nSubject: newTriple.subject, nPredicate: newTriple.predicate, nObject: newTriple.object };
            var newGraph = oldGraph.updateTriple(oldTriple.subject, oldTriple.predicate, oldTriple.object, param);
            this.fileToGraphDict.setValue(newTriple.file, newGraph);
            model.tasks.schedule(new ModelTasks_1.EditTriple(newGraph, file, newTriple.file));
            model.tasks.processAllTasks();
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.editBlock = function (cell, value) {
        var block = cell.getValue();
        var subject;
        // Store prefixmap/prefixes when visualizing the file in the state
        // Transfer prefix to full version
        subject = "TODO";
        var trait = this.cellToTriples.getValue(cell);
        if (trait) {
            var newTrait = new Triple(subject, trait.predicate, trait.object, trait.file);
            this.subjectToBlockDict.remove(trait.subject);
            this.subjectToBlockDict.setValue(subject, block);
            // TODO: CHECK, blockToCellDict zou niet moeten gewijzigd worden
            this.editTriple(cell, trait, newTrait);
        }
        for (var _i = 0, _a = cell.children; _i < _a.length; _i++) {
            var child = _a[_i];
            trait = this.cellToTriples.getValue(child);
            if (trait) {
                var newTrait = new Triple(subject, trait.predicate, trait.object, trait.file);
                this.editTriple(cell, trait, newTrait);
            }
            else {
                console.log("Error: edited cell has no linked triple");
            }
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.handleConformance = function (report) {
        var _this = this;
        var invalidCellsToErrorDict = new Collections.DefaultDictionary(function () { return []; });
        // The keys function of a dictionary returns an array instead of a set, so keep an extra set aswell
        var incInvalidCells = new Collections.Set();
        if (!report.isConforming()) {
            for (var _i = 0, _a = report.getValidationErrors(); _i < _a.length; _i++) {
                var error = _a[_i];
                var block = this.subjectToBlockDict.getValue(error.getDataElement());
                if (block) {
                    var cell = this.blockToCellDict.getValue(block);
                    invalidCellsToErrorDict.getValue(cell).push(error);
                    incInvalidCells.add(cell);
                }
                else {
                    console.log("Error: could not find block for data element: " + error.getDataElement().toString() +
                        "for the conformance error");
                }
            }
        }
        invalidCellsToErrorDict.forEach(function (cell, errors) { return _this.turnCellInvalid(cell, errors); });
        this.invalidCells.difference(incInvalidCells);
        // In invalidCells are now the cells that are no longer invalid
        this.invalidCells.forEach(function (cell) {
            _this.turnCellValid(cell);
        });
        this.invalidCells = incInvalidCells;
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.turnCellInvalid = function (cell, errors) {
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        var model = graph.getModel();
        model.beginUpdate();
        try {
            // Set style of block
            cell.setStyle("InvalidBlock");
            // Set style of rows
            cell.children.forEach(function (rowCell) {
                var found = false;
                for (var _i = 0, errors_1 = errors; _i < errors_1.length; _i++) {
                    var error = errors_1[_i];
                    if (rowCell.value.trait &&
                        rowCell.value.trait.predicate === error.getShapeProperty()) {
                        rowCell.setStyle("InvalidRow");
                        rowCell.value.error = error;
                        found = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if (!found) {
                    rowCell.setStyle("Row");
                    rowCell.value.error = null;
                }
            });
        }
        finally {
            // Updates the display
            model.endUpdate();
            graph.refresh();
        }
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.removeTripleFromBlocks = function (triple) {
        this.blockToCellDict.forEach(function (block) {
            block.traits = block.traits.filter(function (item) { return item !== triple; });
        });
        this.subjectToBlockDict.forEach(function (subject, block) {
            block.traits = block.traits.filter(function (item) { return item !== triple; });
        });
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.turnCellValid = function (cell) {
        var graph = this.state.graph;
        var model = graph.getModel();
        model.beginUpdate();
        try {
            // Set style of block
            cell.setStyle(cell.getValue().blockType);
            // Set style of rows
            cell.children.forEach(function (rowCell) {
                rowCell.setStyle("Row");
                rowCell.value.error = null;
            });
        }
        finally {
            // Updates the display
            model.endUpdate();
            graph.refresh();
        }
    };
    /**
     * Used for checking if user is actively editing or not
     */
    MxGraph.prototype.handleUserAction = function (event) {
        var model = dataAccessProvider_1.DataAccessProvider.getInstance().model;
        // little hack to pass this to a callback
        var self = this;
        // notify that a user action took place
        this.timer.userAction(function () {
            model.tasks.schedule(new ModelTasks_1.GetValidationReport(self));
            // process all tasks when idle
            model.tasks.processAllTasks();
        });
    };
    MxGraph.prototype.render = function () {
        var grid = require('../img/grid.gif');
        return (React.createElement("div", { id: "graphContainer", style: {
                backgroundImage: "url(" + grid + ")",
                cursor: 'default',
                height: '100%',
                overflow: 'auto',
            } }));
    };
    return MxGraph;
}(React.Component));
var Block = /** @class */ (function () {
    function Block(name) {
        this.name = name || "";
        this.realName = name || "";
        this.traits = [];
    }
    Block.prototype.clone = function () {
        return mxUtils.clone(this);
    };
    return Block;
}());
var Triple = /** @class */ (function () {
    function Triple(subject, predicate, object, file) {
        this.subject = subject;
        this.predicate = predicate;
        this.object = object;
        this.file = file;
    }
    Triple.prototype.toString = function () {
        return this.subject + " " + this.predicate + " " + this.object;
    };
    return Triple;
}());
exports.Triple = Triple;
var Row = /** @class */ (function () {
    function Row(name) {
        this.name = name || "";
    }
    Row.prototype.clone = function () {
        return mxUtils.clone(this);
    };
    return Row;
}());
exports.default = MxGraph;
